  <raw>TRAIL OF ATTACKS



KHALID Shaikh Mohammed has been accused of co-ordinating, carrying out, or playing roles in: *  September 11, 2001 terror attacks on the US. *  Last year's October 12 Bali bombings.

Authorities said Mohammed was al-Qaeda's top operative in Asia and must be considered the prime suspect for directing and co-ordinating the attack, carried out by allied Jemaah Islamiyah operatives. *  Plotted with JI in foiled attempt to bomb the Australian and British High Commissions and the US Embassy in Singapore last year. Plot was discovered with the arrest of 17 JI members. *  Fresh plots to attack bridges, power plants and petrol stations in the US, including New York. *  1996 plot to blow up 12 American airliners above the Pacific in a 48-hour period and crash a plane into CIA headquarters in Washington DC. *  Murder last year in Pakistan of Wall Street Journal investigative reporter Daniel Pearl. Mohammed has been accused of slashing Pearl's throat. *  Plots to kill Bill Clinton and the Pope. *  Suicide bombing of the USS Cole in Yemen. *  Foiled attempt last year by Richard Reid to blow up an airliner with a shoe bomb. *  Bombing last year of a synagogue in Tunisia. *  1998 bombings of US embassies in Kenya and Tanzania. *  1993 truck bombing of the World Trade Centre, carried out by his nephew Ramzi Yousef.</raw>
